Language Tag: jp

This character repertoire was derived from the following sources:

- http://www.iana.org/assignments/idn/jp-japanese.html

This document describes the Internationalized Domain Names (IDN) Character Table to be used by NeuLevel in the .BIZ TLD registry for the registration of .BIZ domains in the Japanese language.

NeuLevel would like to thank Japan Registry Services Co., Ltd. (JPRS) for making the .JP IDN language table available on the IANA Repository of TLD IDN Practices.

NeuLevel's Japanese IDN implementation has a feature that mitigates homographic attacks due to Han variants by blocking a name from being registered if a similar name is already registered.

The mechanism by which this works is that every registered domain name has a computed canonical string associated with it. This canonical string is only ever used internally to block similar names from being registered.

The table below lists the characters allowed for registration under the "jp" language tag in the first column. The second column shows the canonical codepoint corresponding to the first column. Due to the differences between this table and the .BIZ Chinese language table, some characters in the second column of this table may not appear in the first column at all. However, this should not affect registrars as the second column is only used internally by the registry and provided as a reference.

This table is in compliance with the ICANN Guidelines for the Implementation of Internationalized Domain Names and is intended for publication in the IANA IDN Character Table Registry.
